## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  [*] --> IDLE
  IDLE --> IN_PROGRESS : BULK_ACTION_SUBMITTED
  IN_PROGRESS --> SUCCESS : BULK_ACTION_SUCCESS
  IN_PROGRESS --> NOT_ALL_SUCCESS : BULK_ACTION_NOT_ALL_SUCCESS
  IN_PROGRESS --> ERROR : BULK_ACTION_ERROR
  ANY_STATE --> IDLE : RESET_BULK_ACTION_STATUS
  note right of ANY_STATE : ANY_STATE represents any current state (IDLE, IN_PROGRESS, SUCCESS, NOT_ALL_SUCCESS, ERROR)
```
